< text>
Consistently okay. Very rarely is there an amazing meal and there are some days where nothing on the menu is above a 6/10, but there has never been a day where everything was bad. Every item is consistently between a 4/10 and a 7/10. There's pizza every day and that's reliably good as well as a salad bar. So don't expect to be blown away, but it's never been too bad.< /text>

< review>
My wife and I have passed by Maggie's Pastry to many times. We just always seem to say "Next time".

Such is life, we are always going to someplace or coming from. We don't often take the time to stop and enjoy.
Today was that time when we made it a point to come in. We were greeted and offered a sample. A incredible pocket of hot potato. It was at that moment that we're were hooked! I began to look around and to be honest it's hard to narrow down what you want, there are soooo many options!
I chose a few things which I can not spell but one had beef and one had jalape√±o and cheese. One was flaky puff pastry wrapped out around meat and of course my all time favorite, RED VELVET!!
I will always have a soft spot for bakers since even though I can bake it's not something I enjoy. I am more of a savory Chef. I know we will be back, thank you for the friendly customer service.</review>

<gmap_id>0x809b21402228ca47:0x610a536592c82232</gmap_id><name>Kirk Banglos<//name>< userid>
113528128156765317196<//userid>
<date>1524334945387< /date><pics>None< /pics>< Text>
This locations has many activities for children and adults. Check out the newsletter, online website or drop on by and take a visit and have a chat with the staff!

Single Adults, Parents & Grandparents have many places to relax while the kids or significant other are browsing the library collection between two floors. Children may also sit and listen during the interactive story telling by volunteers or library staff on scheduled days and hours.

It has air conditioned and heating for those days when needed. Gender Neutral (or as I call it house bathrooms) which are clean and tidy. Even when there are a abundance of children here. Maybe its the parent up bringing!

If your kids or grandkids get a bit cooped up there is a playground right behind the library where they can let go of some steam and energy. The playground ranges from toddler to elementary children under 6 grade.

Literally next door is the recreation and gym complex. If you do come on the weekends be wary that Mahany sports park is also next door and the Soccer games can fill up. Not to mentioned there are 3 baseball fields next door for little leaguers and softball. So parking can be cumbersome on those days or weekend.

Remember this is a library and not Barnes and Noble and a coffee shop so you best be on your absolute and respective behaviour.< /Text>

< text>
The Secret of this tiny little Restaurant is hidden beyond what's available on the menu...

IF THERE WAS A 7 STARS RATING, THIS PLACE DESERVES IT

This is not your conventional pure commercial Sushi Bar... the owner is right there, behind the counter, and talks to you, he asks you what are the flavors you like, and if you let him do his Magic...

WOW... i mean WOWOWOW!!!

What this guy can come up with in a matter of minutes for you it is incredible... the Menu is just to satisfy the common Sushi eaters that go around, but if you ask him to make you something Special off the menu, it will blow you away.

My only Regret:

i live in North Carolina, and i happen to travel for work every once in a while to California... since i discovered this place, any time i visit a Customer in the area, this is a MUST Stop.

I highly recommend this place to all my Friends that travel in that area, so far, everybody has been really happy

This place totally changed my scale of Good in Sushi, because this guy really well far off scale

SIMPLY MAGNIFICENT</text>
